//-------------Hail a taxi---------------
//

:HAILACAB
script_name 'TAXIHL'
set_deatharrest_state 0
const taxi_cost = -10
const taxi_cost_minus_one = 9

:HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
wait $default_wait_time
if
    Player.Defined($player_char)
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
if
    $onmission == 0
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
if and
    is_player_on_foot $player_char
    Player.Money($player_char) > taxi_cost_minus_one
    not Player.WantedLevel($player_char) > 0
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
get_player_coordinates $player_char position_to 0@ 1@ 2@
set_var_float_to_var_float 2@ = 0@
2@ += 10.0
set_var_float_to_var_float 3@ = 1@
3@ += 10.0
set_var_float_to_var_float 4@ = 2@
4@ -= 20.0
set_var_float_to_var_float 5@ = 3@
5@ -= 20.0
get_random_car_of_type_in_area_no_save $cab = get_random_car_with_actors #TAXI in_area 2@ 3@ 4@ 5@
if
    $cab == -1
then
    get_random_car_of_type_in_area_no_save $cab = get_random_car_with_actors #CABBIE in_area 2@ 3@ 4@ 5@
end
if
    $cab == -1
then
    get_random_car_of_type_in_area_no_save $cab = get_random_car_with_actors #KAUFMAN in_area 2@ 3@ 4@ 5@
end
if
    not $cab == -1
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
get_driver_of_car 15@ = car $cab
if
    not 15@ == -1
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
Car.ToggleTaxiLight($cab, True)

:HAILACAB_FOUND
wait 0
if
    Player.Defined($player_char)
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
if
    not Car.Wrecked($cab)
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
get_driver_of_car 15@ = car $cab
if and
    $onmission == 0
    locate_player_on_foot_car_2d $player_char near_car $cab radius 20.0 20.0 0
    not 15@ == -1
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_UNFOUND
if
    is_button_pressed 0 pressed_button 4
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_FOUND

:HAILACAB_BOARD
Car.SetToNormalDriver($cab)
Car.SetMaxSpeed($cab, 0.0)
set_char_wait_state $player_actor anim 16 wait_state_time 800
set_char_obj_enter_car_as_passenger $player_actor go_to_car $cab

:HAILACAB_BOARDING
wait 0
if
    Player.Defined($player_char)
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
if
    not Car.Wrecked($cab)
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
if
    $onmission == 0
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_UNBOARD
if
    not is_char_sitting_in_car $player_actor sitting_in_car $cab
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_BOARDED
get_driver_of_car 15@ = car $cab
if and
    locate_player_on_foot_car_2d $player_char near_car $cab radius 20.0 20.0 0
    not 15@ == -1
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_UNBOARD
if
    not is_button_pressed 0 pressed_button 4
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_BOARD
goto @HAILACAB_BOARDING

:HAILACAB_BOARDED
Car.ToggleTaxiLight($cab, False)
Car.SetToPsychoDriver($cab)
Car.SetMaxSpeed($cab, 100.0)
set_car_driving_style $cab traffic_behavior_to 3
set_fading_colour 0 0 0
fade 0 2000
wait 2000
if
    Player.Defined($player_char)
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
if
    not Car.Wrecked($cab)
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
if
    is_char_sitting_in_car $player_actor sitting_in_car $cab
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
clear_area 0 at -258.372 -403.3983 10.1736 range 5.0
Car.PutAt($cab, -258.372, -403.3983, 10.1736)
Car.Angle($cab) = 29.894
set_car_forward_speed $cab speed_instantly 20.0
Car.SetToNormalDriver($cab)
fade 1 1000
while not is_car_stopped $cab
    if
        Player.Defined($player_char)
    goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
    if
        not Car.Wrecked($cab)
    goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
    if
        is_char_sitting_in_car $player_actor sitting_in_car $cab
    goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
    wait 0
end
set_char_obj_leave_any_car $player_actor
Player.Money($player_char) += taxi_cost
wait 1000
if
    Player.Defined($player_char)
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
if
    not Car.Wrecked($cab)
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
Car.SetToPsychoDriver($cab)
Car.SetMaxSpeed($cab, 100.0)

:HAILACAB_UNFOUND
Car.ToggleTaxiLight($cab, False)
goto @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR

:HAILACAB_UNBOARD
Car.ToggleTaxiLight($cab, False)
Car.SetToPsychoDriver($cab)
Car.SetMaxSpeed($cab, 100.0)
goto @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR

script_name 'NPCWORK'
set_deatharrest_state 0

wait 0
if and
    Player.Defined($player_char)

    $game_saving == 0

    not Car.Wrecked($npc_workers_car)
    not Car.Wrecked($npc_workers_boat)

    10 >= 6@

    15@ == 0

    15@ == 1

    14@ = #GUNBOX
    generate_random_float_in_range 13@ = random_float 0.0 1.0
    if
        13@ > 0.2
    then
        14@ = #WOODENBOX
    end
    if
        13@ > 0.4
    then
        14@ = #BARREL2
    end
    if
        13@ > 0.6
    then
        14@ = #BARREL4
    end
    if
        13@ > 0.8
    then
        14@ = #TRAFFICCONE
    end
    Model.Load(14@)
    while not Model.Available(14@)
        wait 0
        if and
            Player.Defined($player_char)
            $npcs_workers_state == 1
            $game_saving == 0
        goto_if_false @NPC_WORKERS_SCRIPT_END
    end

    Object.RemoveFromMissionCleanupList($npc_workers_box)
    15@++
    TIMERA = 0
end
if and
    15@ == 2
    TIMERA >= 500
then
    set_char_wait_state $npc_worker_2 anim 25 wait_state_time 3000
    15@++
    TIMERA = -200
end
if and
    15@ == 3
    TIMERA >= 0
then
    Actor.Angle($npc_worker_2) = npc_worker_2_start_angle
    cset_lvar_float_to_lvar_int 4@ = integer_to_float TIMERA
    4@ /= 1100.0
    4@ *= 180.0
    cos 4@ = cosine 4@
    4@ += 1.0
    4@ /= 2.0
    5@ = 1.0
    sub_float_var_from_float_var 5@ -= 4@
    3@ = npc_worker_1_end_angle
    3@ -= npc_worker_1_start_angle
    mult_float_lvar_by_float_lvar 3@ *= 5@
    3@ += npc_worker_1_start_angle
    Actor.Angle($npc_worker_1) = 3@
    get_offset_from_char_in_world_coords 0@ 1@ 2@ from_actor $npc_worker_1 offset 0.0 0.9 0.0
    set_object_coordinates $npc_workers_box at 0@ 1@ 2@
    if
        TIMERA >= 1100
    then
        15@++
        TIMERA = 0
    end
end
if
    15@ == 4
then
    clear_all_char_anims $npc_worker_1
    15@++
end
if
    15@ == 5
then
    cset_lvar_float_to_lvar_int 4@ = integer_to_float TIMERA
    4@ /= 500.0
    3@ = npc_worker_2_end_angle
    3@ -= npc_worker_2_start_angle
    mult_float_lvar_by_float_lvar 3@ *= 4@
    3@ += npc_worker_2_start_angle
    Actor.Angle($npc_worker_2) = 3@
    get_offset_from_char_in_world_coords 0@ 1@ 2@ from_actor $npc_worker_2 offset 0.0 0.9 0.0
    set_object_coordinates $npc_workers_box at 0@ 1@ 2@
    if
        TIMERA >= 500
    then
        Object.ToggleInMovingList($npc_workers_box, True)
        generate_random_float_in_range 0@ = random_float -0.5 0.5
        0@ += 0.0
        add_to_object_velocity $npc_workers_box scatter 4.0 0@ 0.0
        Object.RemoveReferences($npc_workers_box)
        15@++
        TIMERA = 0
    end
end

    15@ == 6
    TIMERA >= 600
then
    clear_all_char_anims $npc_worker_2
    generate_random_int_in_range 0@ = random_int_in_ranges 0 200
    15@++
    TIMERA = 0
end

    15@ == 7
    is_int_lvar_greater_than_int_lvar TIMERA > 0@

    15@ = 0
    6@++

:NPC_WORKERS_SCRIPT_LEAVE

    7@ == 0

    set_char_obj_enter_car_as_driver $npc_worker_2 go_to_and_drive_car $npc_workers_car

    $npc_workers_interacted = 1
    7@ = 1

    7@ == 1
    is_char_sitting_in_any_car $npc_worker_1
    is_char_sitting_in_any_car $npc_worker_2
then
    Car.DriveTo($npc_workers_car, -742.9812, -1185.043, 11.0712)
    Car.SetMaxSpeed($npc_workers_car, 10.0)
    7@ = 2
end

    7@ == 2
    locate_car_2d $npc_workers_car sphere 0 near_point -742.9812 -1185.043 radius 2.0 2.0
then
    Car.SetToPsychoDriver($npc_workers_car)
    Car.SetMaxSpeed($npc_workers_car, 15.0)

:DROPMONEY

        $dropped_money_pickups_exist == 1
    then

    not is_player_health_greater $player_char health > 0

    $dropped_money_pickups_exist == 1

    DROPMONEY_DESTROYPICKUPS()

    not Player.Defined($player_char)

:DROPMONEY_WAIT_2

    Player.Defined($player_char)

    Pickup.Picked_up($player_dropped_cash_1)
then
    Pickup.Destroy($player_dropped_cash_1)
else
    Pickup.Destroy($player_dropped_cash_1)
    create_money_pickup $player_dropped_cash_1 = create_cash_pickup 20 at 0@ 1@ 2@
end

    Pickup.Picked_up($player_dropped_cash_2)
then
    Pickup.Destroy($player_dropped_cash_2)
else
    Pickup.Destroy($player_dropped_cash_2)
    create_money_pickup $player_dropped_cash_2 = create_cash_pickup 20 at 3@ 4@ 5@
end

    Pickup.Picked_up($player_dropped_cash_3)
then
    Pickup.Destroy($player_dropped_cash_3)
else
    Pickup.Destroy($player_dropped_cash_3)
    create_money_pickup $player_dropped_cash_3 = create_cash_pickup 20 at 6@ 7@ 8@

:POLICE_CHASES_D
script_name 'PCHASED'
set_deatharrest_state 0
pc_gang_car_model = #CUBAN
pc_step = 0
goto @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT

:POLICE_CHASES_E
script_name 'PCHASEE'
set_deatharrest_state 0
pc_gang_car_model = #ADMIRAL
pc_step = 1000 // only spawn in the night hours
goto @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT

:POLICE_CHASES_SET_GANG_MODELS
if
    pc_gang_car_model == #ADMIRAL
then
    pc_gang_1_model = #CLA
    pc_gang_2_model = #CLB
end
if
    pc_gang_car_model == #GANGBUR
then
    pc_gang_1_model = #CLA
    pc_gang_2_model = #CLB
end
if
    pc_gang_car_model == #CUBAN
then
    pc_gang_1_model = #CBA
    pc_gang_2_model = #CBB
end
if
    pc_gang_car_model == #VOODOO
then
    pc_gang_1_model = #HNA
    pc_gang_2_model = #HNB
end
return

:POLICE_CHASES_WAIT
wait $default_wait_time
if and
    Player.Defined($player_char)
    $allow_police_chases == 1
    $game_saving == 0
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT
get_time_of_day 0@ = hours, 1@ = minutes
if
    pc_step == 1000
then
    if
        2 >= 0@
    goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT
else
    if or
        0@ >= 21
        4 >= 0@
    goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT
end

generate_random_int_in_range 0@ = random_int_in_ranges 1000 60000
TIMERA = 0
while 0@ > TIMERA
    wait $default_wait_time
    if and
        Player.Defined($player_char)
        $allow_police_chases == 1
        $game_saving == 0
    goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT
end

TIMERA = 0
while 10000 > TIMERA
    get_player_coordinates $player_char position_to 4@ 5@ 6@
    generate_random_float_in_range 3@ = random_float 0.0 360.0
    sin 0@ = sine 3@
    0@ *= police_chase_spawn_distance
    add_float_var_to_float_var 0@ += 4@
    cos 1@ = cosine 3@
    1@ *= police_chase_spawn_distance
    add_float_var_to_float_var 1@ += 5@
    get_closest_car_node_with_heading 0@ 1@ 2@ store_nearby_vector_to 0@ 1@ 2@ 3@
    get_distance_between_coords_2d 6@ = distance_between_point 4@ 5@ and_point 0@ 1@
    if
        6@ > police_chase_min_spawn_distance
    then
        if or
            -300.0 > 0@
            0@ > 300.0
            -250.0 > 1@
            1@ > 650.0
        then
            break // don't spawn in Leaf Links
        end
    end
    wait $default_wait_time
    if and
        Player.Defined($player_char)
        $allow_police_chases == 1
        $game_saving == 0
    goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT
end

// there's no opcode to check if a point is in an info zone
4@ = 0 // 1 = Little Havana; 2 = Little Haiti
if and
    -1208.21 < 0@
    0@ < -748.206
    -898.738 < 1@
    1@ < -241.467
then
    4@ = 1
end
if and
    -1208.21 < 0@
    0@ < -578.289
    -241.467 < 1@
    1@ < 412.66
then
    4@ = 2
end
if
    4@ > 0
then
    if or
        pc_gang_car_model == #CUBAN
        pc_gang_car_model == #VOODOO
    goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT
    if
        4@ == 2
    then
        pc_gang_car_model = #VOODOO
    else
        pc_gang_car_model = #CUBAN
    end
else
    if and
        not pc_gang_car_model == #CUBAN
        not pc_gang_car_model == #VOODOO
    goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT
end

POLICE_CHASES_SET_GANG_MODELS()
Model.Load(#POLICE)
Model.Load(#COP)
Model.Load(#UZI)
Model.Load(#MP5LNG)
Model.Load(pc_gang_car_model)
Model.Load(pc_gang_1_model)
Model.Load(pc_gang_2_model)

:POLICE_CHASES_LOAD
if or
    not Model.Available(#POLICE)
    not Model.Available(#COP)
    not Model.Available(#UZI)
    not Model.Available(#MP5LNG)
    not Model.Available(pc_gang_car_model)
    not Model.Available(pc_gang_1_model)
    not Model.Available(pc_gang_2_model)
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_LOADED
wait 0
if and
    Player.Defined($player_char)
    $allow_police_chases == 1
    $game_saving == 0
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT
goto @POLICE_CHASES_LOAD

:POLICE_CHASES_LOADED
Car.Create(pc_police_car_1, #POLICE, 0@, 1@, 2@)
Car.Angle(pc_police_car_1) = 3@
get_offset_from_car_in_world_coords 0@ 1@ 2@ from_car pc_police_car_1 offset 0.0 7.0 0.0
Car.Create(pc_gang_car, pc_gang_car_model, 0@, 1@, 2@)
Car.Angle(pc_gang_car) = 3@
pc_police_car_2 = 0
pc_cop_3 = 0
generate_random_float_in_range 0@ = random_float 0.0 1.0
if
    police_chases_two_police_cars_chance > 0@
then
    get_offset_from_car_in_world_coords 0@ 1@ 2@ from_car pc_police_car_1 offset 0.0 -7.0 0.0
    Car.Create(pc_police_car_2, #POLICE, 0@, 1@, 2@)
    Car.Angle(pc_police_car_2) = 3@
end

Car.Health(pc_police_car_1) = police_chases_police_car_start_health
Car.Health(pc_gang_car) = police_chases_gang_car_start_health
//set_can_burst_car_tyres pc_police_car_1 tires_vulnerable 0
//set_can_burst_car_tyres pc_gang_car tires_vulnerable 0
add_upsidedown_car_check pc_police_car_1
add_upsidedown_car_check pc_gang_car
add_stuck_car_check pc_police_car_1 distance 0.5 time 3000
add_stuck_car_check pc_gang_car distance 0.5 time 3000
create_char_inside_car pc_cop_1 = create_actor 4 #COP in_car pc_police_car_1
create_char_inside_car pc_gang_1 = create_actor 4 pc_gang_1_model in_car pc_gang_car
clear_char_threat_search pc_cop_1
clear_char_threat_search pc_gang_1
set_char_personality pc_cop_1 ped_stats_to 16
set_char_personality pc_gang_1 ped_stats_to 16
set_char_suffers_critical_hits pc_cop_1 dismemberment_possible 0
set_char_suffers_critical_hits pc_gang_1 dismemberment_possible 0
set_char_running pc_cop_1 running 1
set_char_running pc_gang_1 running 1
Actor.Health(pc_cop_1) = 200
Actor.Health(pc_gang_1) = 200
Car.SetMaxSpeed(pc_police_car_1, police_chases_police_car_max_speed)
Car.SetMaxSpeed(pc_gang_car, police_chases_gang_car_max_speed)
set_car_driving_style pc_police_car_1 traffic_behavior_to 2
set_car_driving_style pc_gang_car traffic_behavior_to 2
switch_car_siren pc_police_car_1 siren = 1
set_car_ram_car pc_police_car_1 ram pc_gang_car
Car.SetToPsychoDriver(pc_gang_car)
if
    not Car.Wrecked(pc_police_car_2)
then
    Car.Health(pc_police_car_2) = police_chases_police_car_start_health
    //set_can_burst_car_tyres pc_police_car_2 tires_vulnerable 0
    add_upsidedown_car_check pc_police_car_2
    add_stuck_car_check pc_police_car_2 distance 0.5 time 3000
    create_char_inside_car pc_cop_3 = create_actor 4 #COP in_car pc_police_car_2
    clear_char_threat_search pc_cop_3
    set_char_personality pc_cop_3 ped_stats_to 16
    set_char_suffers_critical_hits pc_cop_3 dismemberment_possible 0
    set_char_running pc_cop_3 running 1
    Actor.Health(pc_cop_3) = 200
    Car.SetMaxSpeed(pc_police_car_2, police_chases_police_car_max_speed)
    set_car_driving_style pc_police_car_2 traffic_behavior_to 2
    switch_car_siren pc_police_car_2 siren = 1
    set_car_ram_car pc_police_car_2 ram pc_gang_car
end

Actor.Create(pc_cop_2, 4, #COP, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0)
Actor.Create(pc_gang_2, 4, pc_gang_2_model, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0)
clear_char_threat_search pc_cop_2
clear_char_threat_search pc_gang_2
set_char_personality pc_cop_2 ped_stats_to 16
set_char_personality pc_gang_2 ped_stats_to 16
set_char_suffers_critical_hits pc_cop_2 dismemberment_possible 0
set_char_suffers_critical_hits pc_gang_2 dismemberment_possible 0
attach_char_to_car pc_cop_2 into_turret_on_car pc_police_car_1 at_car_offset 0.5 0.0 0.8 position 0 angle 180.0 with_weapon 25
attach_char_to_car pc_gang_2 into_turret_on_car pc_gang_car at_car_offset 0.5 0.0 0.8 position 2 angle 180.0 with_weapon 23
set_char_accuracy pc_cop_2 weapon_accuracy_to police_chases_weapon_accuracy_in_car
set_char_accuracy pc_gang_2 weapon_accuracy_to police_chases_weapon_accuracy_in_car
Actor.Health(pc_cop_2) = 200
Actor.Health(pc_gang_2) = 200
set_char_obj_destroy_car pc_cop_2 destroy_car pc_gang_car
set_char_obj_destroy_car pc_gang_2 destroy_car pc_police_car_1

Model.Destroy(#POLICE)
Model.Destroy(#COP)
Model.Destroy(pc_gang_car_model)
Model.Destroy(pc_gang_1_model)
Model.Destroy(pc_gang_2_model)
Model.Destroy(#UZI)
Model.Destroy(#MP5LNG)

1@ = 0 // on foot fight enabled
generate_random_float_in_range 0@ = random_float 0.0 1.0
if
    police_chases_on_foot_fight_chance > 0@
then
    1@ = 1 // will get overwritten for pc_step > 0
end

:POLICE_CHASES_LOOP
wait $default_wait_time
if and
    Player.Defined($player_char)
    $allow_police_chases == 1
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_DESTROY
if
    $game_saving == 0
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_ABANDON

if or
    locate_player_any_means_car_2d $player_char near_car pc_police_car_1 radius police_chase_despawn_distance police_chase_despawn_distance 0
    locate_player_any_means_car_2d $player_char near_car pc_gang_car radius police_chase_despawn_distance police_chase_despawn_distance 0
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_ABANDON
if
    not is_player_in_car $player_char in_car pc_gang_car
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_TAKEOVER
3@ = 0
if
    not Actor.Dead(pc_cop_1)
then
    if
        locate_player_any_means_char_2d $player_char 0 pc_cop_1 radius police_chase_despawn_distance police_chase_despawn_distance
    then
        3@ = 1
    end
end
if and
    3@ == 0
    not Actor.Dead(pc_cop_2)
then
    if
        locate_player_any_means_char_2d $player_char 0 pc_cop_2 radius police_chase_despawn_distance police_chase_despawn_distance
    then
        3@ = 1
    end
end
if and
    3@ == 0
    not Actor.Dead(pc_gang_1)
then
    if
        locate_player_any_means_char_2d $player_char 0 pc_gang_1 radius police_chase_despawn_distance police_chase_despawn_distance
    then
        3@ = 1
    end
end
if and
    3@ == 0
    not Actor.Dead(pc_gang_2)
then
    if
        locate_player_any_means_char_2d $player_char 0 pc_gang_2 radius police_chase_despawn_distance police_chase_despawn_distance
    then
        3@ = 1
    end
end
if
    3@ == 1
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_ABANDON

if or
    pc_step == 0
    pc_step == 1000
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_LOOP_FLEE_POLICE
if and
    not Car.Wrecked(pc_police_car_1)
    not Car.Wrecked(pc_gang_car)
    not Actor.Dead(pc_cop_1)
    not Actor.Dead(pc_cop_2)
    not Actor.Dead(pc_gang_1)
    not Actor.Dead(pc_gang_2)
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_ABANDON
if and
    not Car.Wrecked(pc_police_car_2)
    not Actor.Dead(pc_cop_3)
then
    if or
        not is_car_health_greater pc_police_car_2 health > 249
        is_car_upsidedown pc_police_car_2
    then
        set_char_obj_flee_car pc_cop_3 leave_car pc_police_car_2
    end
    if and
        is_car_stuck pc_police_car_2
        not Actor.Dead(pc_gang_1)
    then
        set_char_obj_kill_char_on_foot pc_cop_3 kill_actor pc_gang_1
    end
end
if
    Car.Wrecked(pc_police_car_2)
then
    set_char_obj_destroy_car pc_gang_2 destroy_car pc_police_car_1
else
    if and
        not locate_char_any_means_car_2d pc_gang_2 near_car pc_police_car_1 radius 15.0 15.0 sphere 0
        locate_char_any_means_car_2d pc_gang_2 near_car pc_police_car_2 radius 15.0 15.0 sphere 0
    then
        set_char_obj_destroy_car pc_gang_2 destroy_car pc_police_car_2
    else
        set_char_obj_destroy_car pc_gang_2 destroy_car pc_police_car_1
    end
end
if
    1@ == 1
then
    if or
        not is_car_health_greater pc_police_car_1 health > 400
        not is_car_health_greater pc_gang_car health > 400
        is_car_upsidedown pc_police_car_1
        is_car_upsidedown pc_gang_car
        is_car_stuck pc_police_car_1
        is_car_stuck pc_gang_car
    then
        goto @POLICE_CHASES_ONFOOT
    end
else
    if or
        not is_car_health_greater pc_police_car_1 health > 249
        is_car_upsidedown pc_police_car_1
    then
        goto @POLICE_CHASES_FLEE_POLICE
    end
    if or
        not is_car_health_greater pc_gang_car health > 249
        is_car_upsidedown pc_gang_car
    then
        goto @POLICE_CHASES_FLEE_GANG
    end
end
goto @POLICE_CHASES_LOOP

:POLICE_CHASES_FLEE_POLICE
Actor.DestroyWithFade(pc_gang_2)
if
    not Car.Wrecked(pc_gang_car)
then
    Car.Health(pc_gang_car) = 1000
end
if
    not Car.Wrecked(pc_police_car_2)
then
    Car.Health(pc_police_car_2) = 1000
    Car.SetToPsychoDriver(pc_police_car_2)
    switch_car_siren pc_police_car_2 siren = 0
end
set_char_obj_flee_car pc_cop_1 leave_car pc_police_car_1
Model.Load(#COP)
while not Model.Available(#COP)
    wait 0
    if and
        Player.Defined($player_char)
        $allow_police_chases == 1
    goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_DESTROY
    if
        $game_saving == 0
    goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_ABANDON
end
POLICE_CHASES_RECREATE_ACTORS_COP()
if
    not Actor.Dead(pc_cop_2)
then
    set_char_obj_flee_on_foot_till_safe pc_cop_2
end
TIMERA = 0
pc_step += 1

:POLICE_CHASES_LOOP_FLEE_POLICE
if or
    pc_step == 1
    pc_step == 1001
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_LOOP_FLEE_GANG
if
    10000 > TIMERA
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_ABANDON_ON_FOOT
//do not combine below 2 ifs, because crashes
if
    not Actor.Dead(pc_cop_1)
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_ABANDON_ON_FOOT
if
    Actor.Driving(pc_cop_1)
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_ABANDON_ON_FOOT
goto @POLICE_CHASES_LOOP

:POLICE_CHASES_FLEE_GANG
Actor.DestroyWithFade(pc_cop_2)
if
    not Car.Wrecked(pc_police_car_1)
then
    Car.Health(pc_police_car_1) = 1000
    Car.SetToPsychoDriver(pc_police_car_1)
    switch_car_siren pc_police_car_1 siren = 0
end
if
    not Car.Wrecked(pc_police_car_2)
then
    Car.Health(pc_police_car_2) = 1000
    Car.SetToPsychoDriver(pc_police_car_2)
    switch_car_siren pc_police_car_2 siren = 0
end
set_char_obj_flee_car pc_gang_1 leave_car pc_gang_car
Model.Load(pc_gang_2_model)
while not Model.Available(pc_gang_2_model)
    wait 0
    if and
        Player.Defined($player_char)
        $allow_police_chases == 1
    goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_DESTROY
    if
        $game_saving == 0
    goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_ABANDON
end
POLICE_CHASES_RECREATE_ACTORS_GANG()
if
    not Actor.Dead(pc_gang_2)
then
    set_char_obj_flee_on_foot_till_safe pc_gang_2
end
TIMERA = 0
pc_step += 2

:POLICE_CHASES_LOOP_FLEE_GANG
if or
    pc_step == 2
    pc_step == 1002
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_LOOP_ON_FOOT
if
    10000 > TIMERA
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_ABANDON_ON_FOOT
//do not combine below 2 ifs, because crashes
if
    not Actor.Dead(pc_gang_1)
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_ABANDON_ON_FOOT
if
    Actor.Driving(pc_gang_1)
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_ABANDON_ON_FOOT
goto @POLICE_CHASES_LOOP

:POLICE_CHASES_ONFOOT
Model.Load(#COP)
Model.Load(#COLT45)
Model.Load(#TEC9)
Model.Load(#UZI)
Model.Load(#MP5LNG)
Model.Load(pc_gang_2_model)

:POLICE_CHASES_ONFOOT_LOAD
if or
    not Model.Available(#COP)
    not Model.Available(#COLT45)
    not Model.Available(#TEC9)
    not Model.Available(#UZI)
    not Model.Available(#MP5LNG)
    not Model.Available(pc_gang_2_model)
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_ONFOOT_LOADED
wait 0
if and
    Player.Defined($player_char)
    $allow_police_chases == 1
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_DESTROY
if
    $game_saving == 0
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_ABANDON
goto @POLICE_CHASES_ONFOOT_LOAD

:POLICE_CHASES_ONFOOT_LOADED
remove_stuck_car_check pc_police_car_1
remove_stuck_car_check pc_gang_car
remove_upsidedown_car_check pc_police_car_1
remove_upsidedown_car_check pc_gang_car
remove_stuck_car_check pc_police_car_2
remove_upsidedown_car_check pc_police_car_2
POLICE_CHASES_RECREATE_ACTORS()
give_weapon_to_char pc_cop_1 weapon 17 ammo 9999
give_weapon_to_char pc_gang_1 weapon 22 ammo 9999
set_char_accuracy pc_cop_1 weapon_accuracy_to police_chases_weapon_accuracy_on_foot
set_char_accuracy pc_gang_1 weapon_accuracy_to police_chases_weapon_accuracy_on_foot
if
    not Actor.Dead(pc_cop_2)
then
    give_weapon_to_char pc_cop_2 weapon 25 ammo 9999
    set_char_accuracy pc_cop_2 weapon_accuracy_to police_chases_weapon_accuracy_on_foot
    set_char_obj_kill_char_on_foot pc_cop_2 kill_actor pc_gang_1
    set_char_obj_kill_char_on_foot pc_gang_1 kill_actor pc_cop_2
end
if
    not Actor.Dead(pc_gang_2)
then
    give_weapon_to_char pc_gang_2 weapon 23 ammo 9999
    set_char_accuracy pc_gang_2 weapon_accuracy_to police_chases_weapon_accuracy_on_foot
    set_char_obj_kill_char_on_foot pc_gang_2 kill_actor pc_cop_1
    set_char_obj_kill_char_on_foot pc_cop_1 kill_actor pc_gang_2
end
if
    not Actor.Dead(pc_cop_3)
then
    give_weapon_to_char pc_cop_3 weapon 17 ammo 9999
    set_char_accuracy pc_cop_3 weapon_accuracy_to police_chases_weapon_accuracy_on_foot
    Actor.Health(pc_cop_3) = 200
    set_char_obj_kill_char_on_foot pc_cop_3 kill_actor pc_gang_1
end

Model.Destroy(#COP)
Model.Destroy(pc_gang_2_model)
Model.Destroy(#COLT45)
Model.Destroy(#TEC9)
Model.Destroy(#UZI)
Model.Destroy(#MP5LNG)
pc_step += 3

:POLICE_CHASES_LOOP_ON_FOOT
if or
    pc_step == 3
    pc_step == 1003
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_LOOP_VICTORY
if or
    not Actor.Dead(pc_cop_1)
    not Actor.Dead(pc_cop_2)
    not Actor.Dead(pc_cop_3)
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_VICTORY
if or
    not Actor.Dead(pc_gang_1)
    not Actor.Dead(pc_gang_2)
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_VICTORY
if
    Actor.Dead(pc_cop_1)
then
    if
        not Actor.Dead(pc_gang_2)
    then
        if
            not Actor.Dead(pc_cop_2)
        then
            set_char_obj_kill_char_on_foot pc_gang_2 kill_actor pc_cop_2
        else
            set_char_obj_kill_char_on_foot pc_gang_2 kill_actor pc_cop_3
        end
    end
end
if
    Actor.Dead(pc_cop_2)
then
    if
        not Actor.Dead(pc_gang_1)
    then
        if
            not Actor.Dead(pc_cop_1)
        then
            set_char_obj_kill_char_on_foot pc_gang_1 kill_actor pc_cop_1
        else
            set_char_obj_kill_char_on_foot pc_gang_1 kill_actor pc_cop_3
        end
    end
end
if
    Actor.Dead(pc_gang_1)
then
    if
        not Actor.Dead(pc_cop_2)
    then
        set_char_obj_kill_char_on_foot pc_cop_2 kill_actor pc_gang_2
    end
    if
        0@ == 1
    then
        set_char_obj_kill_char_on_foot pc_cop_3 kill_actor pc_gang_2
    end
end
if
    Actor.Dead(pc_gang_2)
then
    if
        not Actor.Dead(pc_cop_1)
    then
        set_char_obj_kill_char_on_foot pc_cop_1 kill_actor pc_gang_1
    end
end
goto @POLICE_CHASES_LOOP

:POLICE_CHASES_VICTORY
0@ = 0 // police car 1 boarding
1@ = 0 // police car 2 boarding
2@ = 0 // gang car boarding
if
    not Car.Wrecked(pc_police_car_1)
then
    if
        not Actor.Dead(pc_cop_1)
    then
        set_char_obj_enter_car_as_driver pc_cop_1 go_to_and_drive_car pc_police_car_1
        0@ = 1
    end
    if
        not Actor.Dead(pc_cop_2)
    then
        set_char_obj_enter_car_as_driver pc_cop_2 go_to_and_drive_car pc_police_car_1
        0@ = 1
    end
end
if and
    not Car.Wrecked(pc_police_car_2)
    not Actor.Dead(pc_cop_3)
then
    set_char_obj_enter_car_as_driver pc_cop_3 go_to_and_drive_car pc_police_car_2
    1@ = 1
end
if
    not Car.Wrecked(pc_gang_car)
then
    if

return

:GOLF_PASS
$race_step = -1

$race_time /= 1000
if
    $slomo == 1
then
    TIMERB = -1000
end

:GOLF_PASS_WAIT
if
    $slomo == 0
goto_if_false @GOLF_1
play_mission_passed_tune 1
print_with_number_big 'M_PASS' number 100 time 5000 style 1 // MISSION PASSED! $~1~
Player.Money($player_char) += 100
if
    $passed_golf == 0
then
    register_mission_passed 'GLFMISS'
    player_made_progress 1
    $passed_golf = 1
    Marker.Disable($icon_golf)
    add_short_range_sprite_blip_for_coord $icon_golf = create_icon_marker_without_sphere icon_golf at $golf_x $golf_y $golf_z
    create_clothes_pickup $clothes_pickup_3 = create_clothes_pickup 4 at -240.0 -311.3 10.0
    $clothes_pickup_3_available = 0
    start_new_script @CLOTH3
end
if
    is_int_var_greater_than_int_var $golf_record_seconds > $race_time
then
    register_fastest_time 16 to $race_time
    set_var_int_to_var_int $golf_record_seconds = $race_time
    set_lvar_int_to_var_int 15@ = $race_time
    14@ = 0
    while 15@ > 59
        15@ -= 60
        14@++
    end
    print_with_2_numbers_now 'NEW_REC' 14@ 15@ time 5000 1 // ~g~New Record Set!! ~w~~1~ minutes ~g~and ~w~~1~ seconds.
end
return

:GOLF_CLEANUP
$onmission = 0
if
    $slomo == 1
then
    set_time_scale 1.0
    Camera.Restore_WithJumpCut
    $slomo = 0
end
Marker.Disable($race_marker_1)
Marker.Disable($race_marker_2)
Car.RemoveReferences($race_car)
Object.Destroy($mission_obj_1)
Object.Destroy($mission_obj_2)
Object.Destroy($mission_obj_3)
Object.Destroy($mission_obj_4)
//Object.Destroy($mission_obj_5)
Object.Destroy($mission_obj_6)

Actor.DestroyWithFade($mission_actor_6)
Actor.DestroyWithFade($mission_actor_7)
Actor.DestroyWithFade($mission_actor_8)
Actor.DestroyWithFade($mission_actor_9)

Model.Destroy(#WFOGO)
Model.Destroy(#WATERJUMP1)

//-------------Mission 3---------------
// Special Delivery

:POLICE_1
script_name 'POLICE1'
gosub @POLICE_1_START
if
    has_deatharrest_been_executed
then
    POLICE_1_FAIL()
end
POLICE_1_CLEANUP()
terminate_this_script

:POLICE_1_START
$onmission = 1
register_mission_given
load_mission_text 'POLICE1'
wait 0
Player.CanMove($player_char, False)
set_everyone_ignore_player $player_char ignored_by_everyone_to 1
set_police_ignore_player $player_char ignored_by_cops_state_to 1
set_fading_colour 0 0 0
switch_widescreen 1
Model.Load(#BOBCAT)
Model.Load(#POLICE)
Model.Load(#COP)

:POLICE_1_LOAD
wait 0
if and
    Model.Available(#BOBCAT)
    Model.Available(#POLICE)
    Model.Available(#COP)
goto_if_false @POLICE_1_LOAD
clear_area 0 at 333.704 -501.9003 9.7059 range 5.0
Car.Create($objective_car, #BOBCAT, 333.704, -501.9003, 9.7059)
Car.Angle($objective_car) = 138.7416
clear_area 0 at 359.5053 -514.6687 11.961 range 5.0
Car.Create(0@, #POLICE, 359.5053, -514.6687, 11.961)
Car.Angle(0@) = 322.4988
create_char_inside_car 1@ = create_actor 4 #COP in_car 0@
Car.SetToNormalDriver(0@)
Car.ImmuneToNonPlayer(0@, True)
set_car_temp_action 0@ action 2 time 1700
Camera.SetPosition(364.6485, -526.3016, 13.954, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0)
Camera.PointAt(354.3607, -523.9194, 10.0632, 2)
set_player_coordinates $player_char at 348.0225 -524.783 8.9363
set_player_heading $player_char z_angle_to 237.081
wait 1700
set_interpolation_parameters 0.0 1500
Camera.SetPosition(345.452, -527.0284, 9.0841, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0)
Camera.PointAt(350.2682, -525.0466, 9.9611, 1)
set_char_obj_leave_car 1@ leave_car 0@
TIMERB = 0
while Actor.Driving(1@)
    if
        TIMERB > 5000
    then
        Car.StorePos(0@, 13@, 14@, 15@)
        15@ += 1.0
        warp_char_from_car_to_coord 1@ at 13@ 14@ 15@
        break
    end
    wait 0
end
turn_char_to_face_char $player_actor look_at_actor 1@
turn_char_to_face_char 1@ look_at_actor $player_actor
wait 500
set_char_wait_state 1@ anim 19 wait_state_time 10000
print_now 'INTRO1' time 3000 2
TIMERA = 0
$scene_step = 0

:POLICE_1_INTRO_LOOP
wait 0
if or
    {$I incl.anykey.txt}
then
    goto @POLICE_1_INTRO_END
end

if and
    $scene_step == 0
    TIMERA >= 3000
then
    $scene_step++
    print_now 'INTRO2' time 3000 2
end

if and
    $scene_step == 1
    TIMERA >= 6000
then
    $scene_step++
    print_now 'INTRO3' time 3000 2
    set_interpolation_parameters 0.0 4000
    Camera.SetPosition(330.9225, -525.593, 10.8841, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0)
    Camera.OnVehicle($objective_car, 15, 1)
end

if and
    $scene_step == 2
    TIMERA >= 9000
then
    $scene_step++
    print_now 'INTRO4' time 4000 2
end
if and
    $scene_step == 3
    TIMERA >= 13000
then
    goto @POLICE_1_INTRO_END
end
goto @POLICE_1_INTRO_LOOP

:POLICE_1_INTRO_END
fade 0 1000
wait 1000
clear_prints
Car.Destroy(0@)
Actor.DestroyInstantly(1@)
Model.Destroy(#POLICE)
Model.Destroy(#COP)
Player.CanMove($player_char, True)
set_everyone_ignore_player $player_char ignored_by_everyone_to 0
set_police_ignore_player $player_char ignored_by_cops_state_to 0
switch_widescreen 0
Camera.Restore_WithJumpCut
Camera.SetBehindPlayer
Marker.CreateAboveCar($objective_car_marker, $objective_car)
fade 1 1000
wait 1000
print_now 'GETIN' time 5000 2

:POLICE_1_WAITING_CAR
wait 0
if
    not Car.Wrecked($objective_car)
goto_if_false @POLICE_1_WRECKED
if
    locate_player_any_means_car_2d $player_char near_car $objective_car radius 35.0 35.0 0
goto_if_false @POLICE_1_ABANDONED
if
    is_player_in_car $player_char in_car $objective_car
goto_if_false @POLICE_1_WAITING_CAR
Marker.Disable($objective_car_marker)
add_blip_for_coord $objective_point_marker = create_checkpoint_at -842.6732 -632.8707 10.9397
print_now 'TRAVEL' time 5000 2

:POLICE_1_TRAVEL
wait 0
if
    not Car.Wrecked($objective_car)
goto_if_false @POLICE_1_WRECKED
if
    not is_player_in_car $player_char in_car $objective_car
then
    print_now 'GETBACK' time 5000 2
    Marker.Disable($objective_point_marker)
    Marker.CreateAboveCar($objective_car_marker, $objective_car)
    goto @POLICE_1_WAITING_CAR
end
if
    locate_stopped_player_in_car_3d $player_char stopped 1 -842.6732 -632.8707 10.9397 radius 4.0 4.0 3.0
goto_if_false @POLICE_1_TRAVEL
goto @POLICE_1_PASS
return

:POLICE_1_WRECKED
print_now 'CARF' time 5000 2
POLICE_1_FAIL()
return

:POLICE_1_ABANDONED
print_now 'GONEAWY' time 5000 2
POLICE_1_FAIL()
return

:POLICE_1_FAIL
print_big 'M_FAIL' 5000 ms 1 // MISSION FAILED!
return

:POLICE_1_PASS
play_mission_passed_tune 1
print_with_number_big 'M_PASS' number 100 time 5000 style 1 // MISSION PASSED! $~1~
Player.Money($player_char) += 100
register_mission_passed 'POLIC1S'
player_made_progress 1
$passed_police_1 = 1
Marker.Disable($icon_police)
return

:POLICE_1_CLEANUP
$onmission = 0
Car.RemoveReferences($objective_car)
Marker.Disable($objective_car_marker)
Marker.Disable($objective_point_marker)
Model.Destroy(#BOBCAT)
mission_has_finished
terminate_this_script
